    select
        cast(o.id as varchar) orderId,
        o.code orderCode,
        o.status,
        sup.name supplierName,
        o.quantity,
        o.total_payment totalPayment,
        o.exp_delivery_date expDeliveryDate,
        o.note

        supplier sup

        o.is_deleted = false

            upper(o.code) like concat('%', upper(?), '%')

        sup.name supplierName,

2020-09-06 22:08:48.890 DEBUG 14320 --- [nio-8080-exec-7]  org.hibernate.SQL                        : 
    select
        CAST(p.id as varchar) productId,
        code productCode,
        p.name productName,
        c.name categoryName,
        price,
        image_link linkImg,
        inventory_number warehouseQuantity,
        p.is_deleted ,
        p.description 
    from
        product p 
    left join
        category c 
            on p.category_id = c.id 
    where
        p.is_deleted = false     
        and(
            upper(p.name) like concat('%',upper(?),'%')     
            or upper(c.name ) like concat('%',upper(?),'%')
        )     
    order by
        p.last_updated_stamp DESC limit ?
